{=Gradon (1979) makes no comment about this phrase and her glossary makes it}
{clear that she takes MAKINDE to be a present participle. This would}
{involve reading the prepositional phrase as parenthetical: ´in them}
{who, making by market, leave their benefices´. This reading is however}
{contradicted by her glossing of the term ´maki markat´ as ´strike a}
{bargain´. The BE ´by´ would then be redundant unless MAKINDE is taken}
{to be a verbal noun. See also MED s.v. market n. 3 (a)=}
{.´}
